## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls

# Cross-Org WebIDL to DOM Binding Discovery

## Your Task

Find all WebIDL interface files in `mozilla-firefox/firefox` under `dom/webidl/` that define DOM interfaces for the Fetch API (Request, Response, Headers, FetchEvent). Then find the corresponding C++ binding implementation files under `dom/fetch/` that implement these WebIDL interfaces. Report the WebIDL file, the C++ header, and the C++ implementation file for each Fetch API type.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/firefox--871325b8` (mozilla-firefox/firefox)

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{

  ],

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

Done! I've successfully discovered all the WebIDL interface files and their corresponding C++ binding implementations for the Fetch API types in Firefox. 

Here's what I found:

## Summary of Findings:

**1. Request**
- WebIDL: `dom/webidl/Request.webidl` - Defines the Request interface with properties like method, url, headers, credentials, cache, and redirect
- C++ Header: `dom/fetch/Request.h`
- C++ Implementation: `dom/fetch/Request.cpp`

**2. Response**
- WebIDL: `dom/webidl/Response.webidl` - Defines the Response interface with status, statusText, headers, and static methods
- C++ Header: `dom/fetch/Response.h`
- C++ Implementation: `dom/fetch/Response.cpp`

**3. Headers**
- WebIDL: `dom/webidl/Headers.webidl` - Defines the Headers interface with methods to manage HTTP headers (append, delete, get, set)
- C++ Header: `dom/fetch/Headers.h`
- C++ Implementation: `dom/fetch/Headers.cpp`

**4. FetchEvent**
- WebIDL: `dom/webidl/FetchEvent.webidl` - Defines FetchEvent extending ExtendableEvent with request handling and respondWith() method
- C++ Header: `dom/serviceworkers/ServiceWorkerEvents.h`
- C++ Implementation: `dom/serviceworkers/ServiceWorkerEvents.cpp`

The results are saved in `/workspace/answer.json` with complete file listings and detailed narrative explaining each type's role and location.

Here is the mapping for each type:\\n\\n1. **Request**:\\n   - WebIDL Definition: `dom/webidl/Request.webidl` - Defines the Request interface with properties like method, url, headers, mode, credentials, cache, redirect, and integrity. Implements the Body mixin.\\n   - C++ Header: `dom/fetch/Request.h` - C++ class implementation of the Request interface\\n   - C++ Implementation: `dom/fetch/Request.cpp` - Methods and functionality for the Request class\\n\\n2. **Response**:\\n   - WebIDL Definition: `dom/webidl/Response.webidl` - Defines the Response interface with status, statusText, headers, and various static methods (error, redirect, json). Includes Body mixin.\\n   - C++ Header: `dom/fetch/Response.h` - C++ class implementation of the Response interface\\n   - C++ Implementation: `dom/fetch/Response.cpp` - Methods and functionality for the Response class\\n\\n3. **Headers**:\\n   - WebIDL Definition: `dom/webidl/Headers.webidl` - Defines the Headers interface with methods for managing HTTP headers (append, delete, get, set) and support for iterating over headers.\\n   - C++ Header: `dom/fetch/Headers.h` - C++ class implementation of the Headers interface\\n   - C++ Implementation: `dom/fetch/Headers.cpp` - Methods and functionality for the Headers class\\n\\n4. **FetchEvent**:\\n   - WebIDL Definition: `dom/webidl/FetchEvent.webidl` - Defines the FetchEvent interface that extends ExtendableEvent, with properties for request, clientId, resultingClientId, and methods like respondWith().\\n   - C++ Header: `dom/serviceworkers/ServiceWorkerEvents.h` - C++ class implementation of FetchEvent as part of ServiceWorker event handling\\n   - C++ Implementation: `dom/serviceworkers/ServiceWorkerEvents.cpp` - Methods and functionality for the FetchEvent class\\n\\nThe Request, Response, and Headers implementations are located in the `dom/fetch/` directory as they are core Fetch API types. The FetchEvent implementation is in `dom/serviceworkers/` because it is specific to Service Worker event handling.\"\n}\n",
